    Info

    Welcome to the generated API reference. Get Postman Collection

    Collection

    Class use to define Collection object and information.

    The getAll method.

    This method is use to get all of the painting information from all of the painting in the DB.

    Example request:

    curl -X GET "http://localhost/collection/getall" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/collection/getall",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    Example response:

    {
    "collections": [
        {
            "id": 12,
            "name": "alors la !",
            "description": "ouiiiii",
            "type": 3,
            "created_at": "2018-10-03 09:33:22",
            "updated_at": "2018-10-03 09:33:22"
        },
        {
            "id": 22,
            "name": "dtyh",
            "description": "sqdgv",
            "type": 3,
            "created_at": "2018-10-03 15:49:43",
            "updated_at": "2018-10-03 15:49:43"
        }
    ]
}

    HTTP Request

    GET collection/getall

    The index method.

    This method is use to generate the collection view information.

    You must replace `meowmeowmeow` with your personal API key.

    Example request:

    curl -X GET "http://localhost/collection" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/collection",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    Example response:

    null

    The store method.

    This method is use to store a collection with all its related painting in DB.

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/collection/store" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/collection/store",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    GET painting/freepainting

    painting/cart

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/painting/cart" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/painting/cart",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    GET login

    Handle a login request to the application.

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/login" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/login",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    POST login

    Log the user out of the application.

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/logout" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/logout",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    GET password/reset

    Send a reset link to the given user.

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/password/email" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/password/email",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    POST password/email

    Display the password reset view for the given token.

    If no token is present, display the link request form.

    Example request:

    curl -X GET "http://localhost/password/reset/{token}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/password/reset/{token}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});

    HTTP Request

    GET password/reset/{token}

    Reset the given user's password.

    Example request:

    curl -X POST "http://localhost/password/reset" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
    var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://localhost/password/reset",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
